# Page 5

Meta Title: Lab Grown Diamonds vs Moissanite | Which Is Better?

Meta Description: Compare lab grown diamonds vs moissanite by appearance, sparkle, price, durability, value, certification, engagement rings, earrings, and long-term wear before choosing the right stone.

URL Slug: lab-grown-diamonds-vs-moissanite

# **Lab Grown Diamonds vs Moissanite**

Lab grown diamonds and moissanite are both popular choices for engagement rings and fine jewellery, but they are not the same stone. A lab grown diamond is a real diamond made of carbon, while moissanite is a different gemstone made of silicon carbide. Both can look bright and beautiful, but they differ in sparkle, price, certification, durability, long-term value, and buyer perception.

For buyers comparing lab grown diamonds vs moissanite, the decision usually comes down to one question: do you want a real diamond or a diamond alternative? If you want a real diamond with diamond structure, diamond grading, and diamond appearance, a lab grown diamond is the better choice. If you want a lower-cost stone that looks diamond-like but is not diamond, moissanite may be worth considering.

At Uniglo Diamonds, buyers can explore certified lab grown diamonds, loose lab diamonds, and wholesale lab grown diamond options with clear specifications. This guide explains the difference between lab diamonds and moissanite so buyers can make a confident decision before choosing a loose stone, engagement ring diamond, earrings, or jewellery supply.

## **Quick Answer: Is Lab Grown Diamond Better Than Moissanite?**

A lab grown diamond is better than moissanite if you want a real diamond. Lab grown diamonds are made of carbon and have the same diamond structure as mined diamonds. Moissanite is not diamond; it is a separate gemstone made of silicon carbide. It can be beautiful, bright, and more affordable, but it does not have the same diamond identity, grading system, or market perception.

Moissanite can be a good choice for buyers who want a diamond-like look at a lower price. Lab grown diamonds are a better choice for buyers who want real diamond jewellery, certified loose stones, engagement rings, wholesale diamond supply, or a stone that looks and behaves like a diamond because it is a diamond.

CTA: View Certified Lab Grown Diamonds  
CTA: Compare Loose Lab Diamond Options

## **Lab Grown Diamond vs Moissanite at a Glance**

| Feature | Lab Grown Diamond | Moissanite |
| ----- | ----- | ----- |
| Stone type | Real diamond | Diamond alternative |
| Composition | Carbon | Silicon carbide |
| Same as natural diamond? | Same diamond material, different origin | No |
| Certification | Can be graded as diamond by recognised labs | Not graded as diamond |
| Sparkle style | Diamond brilliance and fire | Strong rainbow-like fire |
| Hardness | Very high | Very high, but not diamond |
| Price | Usually higher than moissanite | Usually lower than lab diamond |
| Best for | Buyers who want a real diamond | Buyers who want a lower-cost diamond-like stone |
| Engagement rings | Excellent choice | Popular alternative |
| Long-term perception | Real diamond | Alternative gemstone |

## **What Is a Lab Grown Diamond?**

A lab grown diamond is a real diamond created in controlled laboratory conditions. It is made of carbon and can be graded by recognised diamond laboratories for cut, colour, clarity, carat weight, measurements, polish, symmetry, fluorescence, and lab grown origin.

Lab grown diamonds are created using advanced processes such as CVD or HPHT. Once grown, the rough diamond is cut and polished like a natural diamond. The final stone can be used in engagement rings, earrings, pendants, bracelets, loose diamond purchases, and wholesale jewellery production.

The key point is simple: lab grown diamonds are real diamonds. Their origin is different from mined diamonds, but their diamond identity is real.

## **What Is Moissanite?**

Moissanite is a gemstone made of silicon carbide. It is not diamond, but it is often used as a diamond alternative because it is bright, durable, and usually more affordable than diamond. Moissanite has its own look, sparkle, and value structure.

Many buyers like moissanite because it gives a large and bright appearance at a lower price. However, moissanite does not have the same chemical composition as diamond and is not graded as a diamond. It can look similar from a distance, but side by side, many people notice differences in sparkle, fire, and overall appearance.

## **Lab Grown Diamonds vs Moissanite: The Main Difference**

The biggest difference is material. A lab grown diamond is carbon. Moissanite is silicon carbide. This matters because the two stones behave differently, sparkle differently, and are viewed differently by buyers.

Lab grown diamonds are chosen by people who want a genuine diamond without choosing a mined stone. Moissanite is chosen by people who want a diamond-like stone without paying diamond prices.

| Difference | Why It Matters |
| ----- | ----- |
| Lab grown diamonds are real diamonds | Important for engagement rings and fine jewellery buyers |
| Moissanite is not diamond | Important for buyers who want true diamond identity |
| Lab diamonds can be diamond certified | Helps compare quality and specifications |
| Moissanite has different sparkle | Some buyers like it, others find it too rainbow-like |
| Moissanite usually costs less | Good for budget-focused buyers |
| Lab diamonds have stronger diamond perception | Better for buyers who specifically want diamonds |

## **Lab Grown Diamond vs Moissanite: Appearance**

Lab grown diamonds and moissanite can both look beautiful, but they do not look exactly the same. Lab grown diamonds have the classic diamond appearance that buyers expect from engagement rings and fine jewellery. Moissanite can look very bright, but its sparkle often has more rainbow flashes.

Some buyers love moissanite’s fire because it appears very lively under light. Other buyers feel that moissanite looks less diamond-like, especially in larger sizes. Lab grown diamonds usually look closer to natural diamonds because they are diamonds.

| Appearance Factor | Lab Grown Diamond | Moissanite |
| ----- | ----- | ----- |
| Overall look | Diamond-like because it is diamond | Diamond-like but different |
| White sparkle | Classic diamond brilliance | Bright, sometimes sharper |
| Rainbow fire | Present in diamond style | Often stronger and more noticeable |
| Larger stones | Looks like a diamond when well cut | Differences may become easier to see |
| Side-by-side comparison | More natural diamond-like | Can show more colourful flashes |
| Best for buyers who want | A real diamond look | A bright alternative look |

## **Lab Grown Diamond vs Moissanite: Sparkle**

Sparkle is one of the biggest reasons buyers compare these two stones. A lab grown diamond has diamond brilliance, fire, and scintillation. Moissanite has a different optical performance and often shows more rainbow-like fire.

This does not mean one is beautiful and the other is not. Both can be attractive. The difference is style. If you want the traditional diamond sparkle, lab grown diamond is the better match. If you want a very fiery, colourful sparkle and are comfortable with a non-diamond stone, moissanite may appeal to you.

| Sparkle Question | Lab Grown Diamond | Moissanite |
| ----- | ----- | ----- |
| Which sparkles like a diamond? | Lab grown diamond | Similar but not identical |
| Which has more rainbow fire? | Less than moissanite | Usually more |
| Which looks more traditional? | Lab grown diamond | Moissanite may look more colourful |
| Which is better for classic engagement rings? | Lab grown diamond | Depends on preference |
| Which may look different in large sizes? | Usually more diamond-like | Differences can be more visible |

## **Lab Grown Diamond vs Moissanite: Price**

Moissanite is usually cheaper than lab grown diamond. This is one reason many buyers consider it. If the main goal is getting a large centre stone at the lowest possible price, moissanite may look attractive.

However, lower price does not mean it is the same product. A lab grown diamond costs more because it is a real diamond. It can be graded as a diamond, certified as a diamond, and compared using diamond quality standards. Moissanite has its own pricing and grading structure.

| Price Factor | Lab Grown Diamond | Moissanite |
| ----- | ----- | ----- |
| Usually cheaper? | No | Yes |
| Real diamond pricing? | Yes | No |
| Best for low budget | Good, but usually more than moissanite | Strong |
| Best for diamond buyers | Strong | Not ideal |
| Best for large look at lower cost | Good | Very strong |
| Best for certified diamond purchase | Strong | Not a diamond certificate |

## **Why Lab Grown Diamonds Cost More Than Moissanite**

Lab grown diamonds cost more than moissanite because they are real diamonds. They require diamond growth, cutting, polishing, grading, and certification. Moissanite is a different gemstone with a different production process and market value.

A buyer should not compare only size and price. A 2 carat-looking moissanite may cost less than a 2 carat lab grown diamond, but it is not a 2 carat diamond. It is a different gemstone with a different identity.

| Reason | Explanation |
| ----- | ----- |
| Lab grown diamond is real diamond | It carries diamond identity and grading |
| Diamond cutting standards apply | Cut quality affects brilliance and value |
| Certification may apply | IGI or GIA grading can support comparison |
| Moissanite is a different stone | It is priced differently from diamond |
| Buyer perception differs | Diamond buyers usually value lab diamonds more than moissanite |

## **Lab Grown Diamond vs Moissanite: Durability**

Both lab grown diamonds and moissanite are durable enough for jewellery, including engagement rings. Lab grown diamonds are diamonds, so they are extremely hard and suitable for daily wear. Moissanite is also very durable and commonly used in rings.

However, hardness is not the only factor. A ring can still be damaged if the setting is weak or if the stone is hit hard. Proper setting, cleaning, and care matter for both stones.

| Durability Factor | Lab Grown Diamond | Moissanite |
| ----- | ----- | ----- |
| Suitable for daily wear | Yes | Yes |
| Suitable for engagement rings | Yes | Yes |
| Scratch resistance | Extremely high | Very high |
| Can chip if hit hard? | Yes | Yes |
| Needs proper setting | Yes | Yes |
| Long-term jewellery use | Excellent | Very good |

## **Lab Grown Diamond vs Moissanite: Certification**

Lab grown diamonds can be certified by recognised diamond laboratories. A certificate can show carat weight, colour, clarity, cut details, measurements, polish, symmetry, fluorescence, and lab grown origin. This makes lab grown diamonds easier to compare, especially for loose stones and important purchases.

Moissanite is not graded like diamond. It may come with product information or quality descriptions, but it is not a diamond and should not be presented as one. This matters when buyers want transparency and long-term confidence.

| Certification Factor | Lab Grown Diamond | Moissanite |
| ----- | ----- | ----- |
| Diamond grading report | Available | Not applicable |
| IGI/GIA diamond report | Can be available | Not applicable as diamond |
| 4Cs comparison | Yes | Different system |
| Origin confirmation | Lab grown origin can be stated | Moissanite identity stated separately |
| Best for certified diamond buyers | Yes | No |

## **Lab Grown Diamond vs Moissanite: Engagement Rings**

For engagement rings, the choice depends on personal preference and budget. Lab grown diamonds are better for couples who want a real diamond engagement ring. Moissanite is better for couples who want a larger, lower-cost stone and are comfortable choosing a diamond alternative.

A lab grown diamond engagement ring will be viewed as a diamond ring because the centre stone is a diamond. A moissanite engagement ring can still be meaningful and beautiful, but it is not a diamond ring.

| Engagement Ring Priority | Better Choice |
| ----- | ----- |
| Real diamond centre stone | Lab grown diamond |
| Lowest price for large look | Moissanite |
| Classic diamond appearance | Lab grown diamond |
| Strong rainbow sparkle | Moissanite |
| Diamond certificate | Lab grown diamond |
| Bigger stone for very low budget | Moissanite |
| Long-term diamond perception | Lab grown diamond |
| Alternative gemstone preference | Moissanite |

## **Lab Grown Diamond vs Moissanite for Earrings**

Both stones can be used in earrings, but lab grown diamonds are better for buyers who want real diamond earrings. Moissanite earrings can be bright and budget-friendly, but they may have a different sparkle style.

For stud earrings, buyers often want matching stones. Lab grown diamonds can be selected by carat, colour, clarity, and certificate for larger stones. Moissanite can be selected for size and appearance, but it does not carry the same diamond grading structure.

| Earring Type | Lab Grown Diamond | Moissanite |
| ----- | ----- | ----- |
| Stud earrings | Excellent for real diamond studs | Good for lower-cost bright studs |
| Bridal earrings | Strong diamond choice | Good alternative |
| Daily earrings | Durable and refined | Durable and bright |
| Luxury earrings | Better diamond perception | Less diamond-like |
| Matched pairs | Can be matched by diamond grades | Matched by moissanite specifications |

## **Lab Grown Diamond vs Moissanite for Pendants**

For pendants, both stones can work depending on the desired look. A lab grown diamond pendant gives a real diamond appearance and can be certified if the stone is large enough or important enough for the buyer. A moissanite pendant can provide a large, bright look at a lower cost.

If the buyer wants a classic solitaire diamond pendant, lab grown diamond is the better fit. If the buyer wants a bright necklace at a lower price and does not mind that it is not diamond, moissanite can work.

| Pendant Priority | Better Choice |
| ----- | ----- |
| Real diamond pendant | Lab grown diamond |
| Lower-cost large pendant | Moissanite |
| Classic luxury appearance | Lab grown diamond |
| Strong rainbow fire | Moissanite |
| Certified centre stone | Lab grown diamond |

## **Lab Grown Diamond vs Moissanite for Jewellery Businesses**

For jewellers, retailers, and manufacturers, lab grown diamonds and moissanite serve different customers. Lab grown diamonds are suitable for customers who want real diamond jewellery at more accessible pricing than natural diamonds. Moissanite is suitable for customers who want a lower-cost alternative.

A jewellery business should clearly label and explain both. Misrepresenting moissanite as diamond can damage trust. If a customer asks for diamond, lab grown diamond is the better alternative to natural diamond. If a customer asks for a diamond-like stone at lower cost, moissanite can be offered separately.

| Business Use | Lab Grown Diamond | Moissanite |
| ----- | ----- | ----- |
| Diamond engagement rings | Strong | Not diamond |
| Affordable fine jewellery | Strong | Good alternative |
| Wholesale diamond supply | Strong | Different category |
| Certified loose stones | Strong | Not diamond grading |
| Low-cost alternative collections | Possible | Strong |
| Customer trust | Must be clearly disclosed | Must be clearly disclosed |

## **Lab Grown Diamond vs Moissanite: Value**

Value depends on what the buyer wants. If value means getting a real diamond with better size-for-budget than natural diamond, lab grown diamonds are a strong choice. If value means getting the largest bright stone at the lowest price, moissanite may be the better choice.

For engagement rings and fine jewellery, many buyers prefer lab grown diamonds because they want the stone to be a diamond. Moissanite is valuable as an alternative, but it does not carry the same identity as diamond.

| Alternative gemstone choice | Moissanite |

## **Lab Grown Diamond vs Moissanite: Resale**

Neither lab grown diamonds nor moissanite should be bought mainly as an investment. Lab grown diamonds usually have lower resale value than natural diamonds, and moissanite also has limited resale demand compared with diamonds.

If resale matters strongly, buyers should study the secondary market carefully. If the goal is to wear and enjoy the stone, then the better choice depends on whether the buyer wants a real diamond or a diamond alternative.

| Resale Question | Lab Grown Diamond | Moissanite |
| ----- | ----- | ----- |

| Best bought as investment? | Usually no | No |

| Best bought for wearing? | Yes | Yes |
| Buyer should understand resale? | Yes | Yes |

## **Lab Grown Diamond vs Moissanite: Which Looks More Like a Natural Diamond?**

Lab grown diamond looks more like natural diamond because it is diamond. If a lab grown diamond and a natural diamond have similar grades and cut quality, they can look nearly identical to the naked eye.

Moissanite can look diamond-like, but it has a different sparkle pattern. In larger sizes, the difference can become easier to notice, especially because moissanite often shows more rainbow fire.

| Natural Diamond-Like Factor | Better Choice |
| ----- | ----- |
| Same material as natural diamond | Lab grown diamond |
| Same diamond sparkle style | Lab grown diamond |
| Same diamond grading structure | Lab grown diamond |
| Similar look from distance | Both can appear similar |
| More rainbow fire | Moissanite |
| Best natural diamond alternative | Lab grown diamond |

## **Lab Grown Diamond vs Moissanite: Pros and Cons**

Both options have strengths. Lab grown diamonds offer real diamond identity, certification, and classic appearance. Moissanite offers lower cost, strong brightness, and a diamond-like look for buyers who do not need a real diamond.

| Stone | Pros | Cons |

## **Who Should Choose a Lab Grown Diamond?**

You should choose a lab grown diamond if you want a real diamond and want better value than a natural diamond. It is a strong option for engagement rings, loose diamond buying, earrings, pendants, and wholesale jewellery sourcing.

Lab grown diamonds are especially suitable for buyers who want certification, clear grading, and diamond identity. If you are asking, “Is this a real diamond?” then lab grown is usually the safer choice over moissanite.

## **Who Should Choose Moissanite?**

You should choose moissanite if your main goal is a bright, durable, diamond-like stone at a lower price. Moissanite is a good option for buyers who do not need the stone to be a diamond.

Moissanite may also work well for fashion jewellery, budget engagement rings, travel rings, or buyers who like its rainbow-like sparkle. The important thing is to understand that moissanite is not a diamond.

## **How to Choose Between Lab Grown Diamond and Moissanite**

The easiest way to choose is to decide whether diamond identity matters to you. If you want a real diamond, choose lab grown diamond. If you only want a diamond-like look and price is the main priority, moissanite may be acceptable.

After that, think about jewellery purpose. For an engagement ring, many buyers prefer lab grown diamonds because the ring remains a diamond ring. For fashion jewellery or lower-budget pieces, moissanite can be a practical alternative.

| Question | If Your Answer Is Yes |

| Am I okay with a diamond alternative? | Consider moissanite |
| Do I need loose diamonds for jewellery production? | Choose lab grown diamond |
| Do I need a lower-cost fashion stone? | Consider moissanite |

## **Common Mistakes When Comparing Lab Grown Diamonds and Moissanite**

The biggest mistake is thinking lab grown diamonds and moissanite are the same. They are not. Lab grown diamonds are real diamonds. Moissanite is a diamond alternative.

Another mistake is comparing only price. Moissanite usually costs less, but that does not make it the same value as a diamond. Buyers should compare purpose, identity, appearance, certification, and long-term expectations.

| Mistake | Better Approach |
| ----- | ----- |
| Thinking moissanite is a lab diamond | Understand they are different stones |

| Ignoring sparkle difference | Compare appearance in different lighting |
| Buying moissanite when you want diamond | Choose lab grown diamond |
| Buying lab diamond when you only want lowest cost | Consider moissanite |
| Not checking supplier disclosure | Make sure the stone is clearly identified |

# **Lab Grown Diamonds vs Moissanite FAQs**

## **Basic FAQs**

### **Is moissanite the same as a lab grown diamond?**

No, moissanite is not the same as a lab grown diamond. A lab grown diamond is made of carbon and is a real diamond. Moissanite is made of silicon carbide and is a different gemstone.

### **Is a lab grown diamond real?**

Yes, a lab grown diamond is real diamond. It has diamond structure and can be graded as a diamond. Its origin is laboratory-grown rather than mined.

### **Is moissanite a real diamond?**

No, moissanite is not a real diamond. It is a diamond alternative that can look similar but has a different composition and sparkle.

### **Is moissanite fake?**

Moissanite is not fake if it is sold correctly as moissanite. It is a real gemstone, but it is not diamond.

### **Is lab grown diamond fake?**

No, lab grown diamond is not fake. It is a real diamond created in controlled laboratory conditions.

### **Which is better, lab grown diamond or moissanite?**

Lab grown diamond is better if you want a real diamond. Moissanite is better if you want a lower-cost diamond alternative and do not need the stone to be diamond.

### **Why do people compare lab grown diamonds and moissanite?**

People compare them because both are popular alternatives to natural diamonds. However, lab grown diamonds are real diamonds, while moissanite is a different gemstone.

### **Can people tell moissanite from lab grown diamond?**

Some people can notice the difference, especially in larger stones or certain lighting. Moissanite often shows more rainbow-like fire than diamond.

## **Appearance and Sparkle FAQs**

### **Does moissanite look like a lab grown diamond?**

Moissanite can look similar from a distance, but it does not look exactly the same. It often has stronger rainbow fire and a different sparkle pattern.

### **Which sparkles more, lab grown diamond or moissanite?**

Moissanite often shows more rainbow-like fire, while lab grown diamonds show classic diamond brilliance and sparkle.

### **Which looks more like a natural diamond?**

Lab grown diamond looks more like a natural diamond because it is diamond. Moissanite is a diamond alternative and may look different, especially side by side.

### **Does moissanite look too sparkly?**

Some buyers feel moissanite looks too fiery or rainbow-like, especially in larger stones. Others love this effect. It depends on personal preference.

### **Does lab grown diamond sparkle like a natural diamond?**

Yes, a well-cut lab grown diamond can sparkle like a natural diamond because both are diamonds.

### **Does moissanite get cloudy?**

Moissanite does not usually become cloudy simply because it is moissanite, but like all jewellery stones, it can collect dirt and oils and should be cleaned.

### **Does lab grown diamond get cloudy?**

A properly grown and cut lab grown diamond does not become cloudy simply because it is lab grown. It should be cleaned like any diamond jewellery.

## **Price FAQs**

### **Is moissanite cheaper than lab grown diamond?**

Yes, moissanite is usually cheaper than lab grown diamond because it is not diamond and has a different value structure.

### **Why is lab grown diamond more expensive than moissanite?**

Lab grown diamond is more expensive because it is a real diamond, can be graded as a diamond, and carries diamond identity and certification.

### **Is lab grown diamond worth the extra money over moissanite?**

It is worth it if you want a real diamond. If you only want a bright diamond-like stone at the lowest price, moissanite may be enough.

### **Is moissanite better value than lab grown diamond?**

Moissanite may be better value if your goal is low price and large appearance. Lab grown diamond is better value if your goal is a real diamond at a more accessible price than natural diamond.

### **Should I buy moissanite to save money?**

You can buy moissanite to save money if you are comfortable with a non-diamond gemstone. If you want diamond identity, choose lab grown diamond.

### **Are lab grown diamonds expensive?**

Lab grown diamonds usually cost more than moissanite but less than natural diamonds with similar visible specifications.

## **Durability FAQs**

### **Is lab grown diamond more durable than moissanite?**

Lab grown diamond is diamond and has extremely high hardness. Moissanite is also very durable, but it is not diamond.

### **Can moissanite be worn every day?**

Yes, moissanite can be worn every day if it is set properly and cared for.

### **Can lab grown diamonds be worn every day?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds are suitable for daily wear, including engagement rings.

### **Can moissanite scratch?**

Moissanite is very scratch-resistant, but it is not the same as diamond. Proper care is still important.

### **Can lab grown diamonds chip?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds can chip if hit hard in the wrong way, just like natural diamonds. A secure setting helps protect the stone.

## **Engagement Ring FAQs**

### **Is lab grown diamond better than moissanite for engagement rings?**

Lab grown diamond is better if you want a real diamond engagement ring. Moissanite is better if you want a lower-cost alternative stone.

### **Is moissanite okay for an engagement ring?**

Yes, moissanite can be used in engagement rings, but it should be understood as a diamond alternative, not a diamond.

### **Will people know my ring is moissanite?**

Some people may not notice, but others may see the difference because moissanite has a different sparkle pattern.

### **Will people know my ring is lab grown diamond?**

Most people cannot tell a lab grown diamond from a natural diamond by eye when the stone is well cut and properly selected.

### **Is a lab grown diamond engagement ring real?**

Yes, a lab grown diamond engagement ring has a real diamond centre stone if the stone is properly disclosed as lab grown diamond.

### **Is a moissanite engagement ring less valuable?**

Moissanite usually has a lower value than diamond. However, it can still be meaningful and beautiful if the buyer chooses it knowingly.

## **Certification FAQs**

### **Can lab grown diamonds be certified?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds can be certified by recognised grading laboratories.

### **Can moissanite be diamond certified?**

No, moissanite cannot be certified as a diamond because it is not diamond. It may come with product information or gemstone documentation, but not a diamond grading report.

### **Is IGI certification available for lab grown diamonds?**

Yes, IGI certification is commonly available for lab grown diamonds and helps buyers compare specifications.

### **Is GIA certification available for lab grown diamonds?**

Yes, GIA certification can be available for lab grown diamonds. Buyers should check the actual report details.

### **Should I buy certified lab grown diamonds?**

Yes, certification is recommended for important purchases because it confirms the diamond’s specifications and lab grown origin.

### **Do I need certification for moissanite?**

Moissanite does not use diamond grading certification. Buyers should still ask for clear stone details and supplier transparency.

## **Value and Resale FAQs**

### **Does lab grown diamond hold value better than moissanite?**

Lab grown diamonds usually have stronger diamond perception than moissanite, but both generally have weaker resale expectations than natural diamonds.

### **Is moissanite good for resale?**

Moissanite usually has limited resale demand compared with diamonds. It is best bought for wearing rather than resale.

### **Is lab grown diamond good for resale?**

Lab grown diamonds usually have lower resale value than natural diamonds. They are best bought for beauty, jewellery use, and value at purchase.

### **Should I buy lab grown diamond as an investment?**

Usually no. Lab grown diamonds are better purchased for jewellery use, not investment resale.

### **Should I buy moissanite as an investment?**

No, moissanite is not usually bought as an investment. It is best purchased as an affordable jewellery stone.

## **Buying FAQs**

### **Should I buy lab grown diamond or moissanite?**

Buy lab grown diamond if you want a real diamond. Buy moissanite if you want a lower-cost diamond alternative.

### **What should I check before buying a lab grown diamond?**

Check shape, carat, cut, colour, clarity, certificate, measurements, price, and supplier trust.

### **What should I check before buying moissanite?**

Check size, cut, colour appearance, setting quality, supplier transparency, and whether the stone is clearly disclosed as moissanite.

### **Where can I buy certified lab grown diamonds?**

You can buy certified lab grown diamonds from a supplier that provides clear specifications, certificates, current availability, and support before purchase.

### **Can I buy loose lab grown diamonds?**

Yes, loose lab grown diamonds are available for engagement rings, earrings, pendants, bracelets, custom jewellery, and wholesale sourcing.

### **Can jewellers buy lab grown diamonds wholesale?**

Yes, jewellers, retailers, designers, and manufacturers can source lab grown diamonds wholesale for jewellery production and resale.

## **Final Summary**

Lab grown diamonds and moissanite are both popular, but they are not the same. A lab grown diamond is a real diamond made of carbon. Moissanite is a different gemstone made of silicon carbide. Moissanite is usually cheaper and very bright, but lab grown diamond is the better choice for buyers who want a real diamond.

For engagement rings, fine jewellery, certified loose stones, and wholesale diamond sourcing, lab grown diamonds offer stronger diamond identity, clearer certification, and a more traditional diamond appearance. Moissanite can be a good alternative for buyers who want a lower-cost stone and are comfortable choosing something other than diamond.

Uniglo Diamonds helps buyers source certified lab grown diamonds with clear specifications, current availability, and support for loose diamond and wholesale enquiries.

# page 6

Meta Title: Are Lab Grown Diamonds Real? Complete Buyer Guide

Meta Description: Yes, lab grown diamonds are real diamonds. Learn how lab grown diamonds are made, how they compare to natural diamonds, whether they test as real, and what to check before buying certified lab diamonds.

URL Slug: are-lab-grown-diamonds-real

# **Are Lab Grown Diamonds Real?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds are real diamonds. They are not fake diamonds, cubic zirconia, glass, crystal, or moissanite. A lab grown diamond is made of carbon and has the same basic diamond structure as a natural diamond. The main difference is origin: a natural diamond forms underground, while a lab grown diamond is created in controlled laboratory conditions using advanced technology.

This question is one of the most common concerns buyers have before choosing a lab grown diamond. Many people hear the word “lab” and assume the diamond must be artificial in the same way as a simulant, but that is not correct. A lab grown diamond is artificial in origin, but it is not a fake diamond. It is a real diamond created through a different process.

At Uniglo Diamonds, buyers can explore certified lab grown diamonds with clear specifications, grading reports, and support for loose lab diamond sourcing. This guide explains what makes lab grown diamonds real, how they are made, how they compare with natural diamonds, whether they pass diamond testers, and what buyers should check before buying one.

## **Quick Answer: Are Lab Grown Diamonds Real?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds are real diamonds because they are made of carbon and have diamond properties. They can be cut, polished, graded, certified, and used in engagement rings, earrings, pendants, bracelets, and fine jewellery just like natural diamonds.

The only major difference is origin. Natural diamonds are formed inside the earth over a very long period of time, while lab grown diamonds are created above ground using CVD or HPHT technology. A lab grown diamond is not a diamond imitation. It is a real diamond with a laboratory-grown origin.

CTA: View Certified Lab Grown Diamonds  
CTA: Request Lab Diamond Availability

## **Lab Grown Diamonds at a Glance**

| Question | Direct Answer |
| ----- | ----- |
| Are lab grown diamonds real? | Yes, they are real diamonds. |
| Are lab grown diamonds fake? | No, they are not fake diamonds. |
| Are lab grown diamonds natural? | No, they are not natural diamonds. |
| Are lab grown diamonds moissanite? | No, moissanite is a different gemstone. |
| Are lab grown diamonds cubic zirconia? | No, cubic zirconia is a diamond simulant. |
| Do lab grown diamonds test as diamonds? | Many standard diamond testers identify them as diamonds, but specialist testing confirms origin. |
| Can lab grown diamonds be certified? | Yes, they can be certified by recognised grading laboratories. |
| Can lab grown diamonds be used in engagement rings? | Yes, they are commonly used in engagement rings and fine jewellery. |

## **What Makes a Lab Grown Diamond a Real Diamond?**

A diamond is defined by its structure and material, not only by where it came from. A lab grown diamond is made of carbon atoms arranged in a diamond crystal structure. This is why it can have the same brilliance, hardness, fire, and sparkle associated with diamonds.

A fake diamond, on the other hand, is a material that only imitates the look of diamond. Cubic zirconia and glass may look bright at first, but they are not diamonds. Moissanite is a real gemstone, but it is not diamond because it is made of silicon carbide, not carbon.

| Stone Type | Is It a Real Diamond? | Material | Main Difference |
| ----- | ----- | ----- | ----- |
| Lab grown diamond | Yes | Carbon | Created in a laboratory |
| Natural diamond | Yes | Carbon | Formed underground |
| Moissanite | No | Silicon carbide | Diamond alternative |
| Cubic zirconia | No | Zirconium dioxide | Diamond simulant |
| Glass/crystal | No | Various materials | Imitation stone |

## **Why Do People Think Lab Grown Diamonds Are Fake?**

Many buyers think lab grown diamonds are fake because the word “lab” sounds artificial. This creates confusion. A lab grown diamond is created artificially, but the final stone is still a real diamond. Its origin is man-made, but its material is diamond.

The confusion also comes from the jewellery market using many similar terms. Lab grown diamond, lab created diamond, simulated diamond, moissanite, cubic zirconia, synthetic diamond, and diamond alternative are often mixed together by buyers. But these terms do not all mean the same thing.

A lab grown diamond is real diamond. A simulated diamond is not diamond. Moissanite is not diamond. Cubic zirconia is not diamond. This distinction is very important for buyers.

| Term | Meaning |
| ----- | ----- |
| Lab grown diamond | Real diamond grown in a controlled environment |
| Lab created diamond | Another term for lab grown diamond |
| Synthetic diamond | Technical term sometimes used for lab grown diamond |
| Simulated diamond | A stone that imitates diamond but is not diamond |
| Moissanite | A different gemstone used as a diamond alternative |
| Cubic zirconia | A low-cost diamond simulant |
| Natural diamond | A real diamond formed underground |

## **Lab Grown Diamonds vs Fake Diamonds**

A fake diamond is usually a material that looks like a diamond but does not have diamond properties. Lab grown diamonds should not be grouped with fake diamonds because they are real diamonds.

The best way to understand this is simple: lab grown diamonds are not trying to imitate diamond. They are diamonds. Cubic zirconia and glass imitate diamond. Moissanite is a different gemstone that can resemble diamond, but it is still not diamond.

| Feature | Lab Grown Diamond | Fake Diamond / Simulant |
| ----- | ----- | ----- |
| Made of carbon | Yes | No |
| Real diamond structure | Yes | No |
| Can be diamond certified | Yes | No |
| Used in fine jewellery | Yes | Sometimes, but not as diamond |
| Diamond tester result | Often tests as diamond | Usually does not test as diamond, depending on material |
| Long-term buyer perception | Real diamond | Imitation or alternative |

## **Lab Grown Diamonds vs Natural Diamonds**

Lab grown diamonds and natural diamonds are both real diamonds. The difference is origin. A natural diamond is mined from the earth. A lab grown diamond is created in a laboratory. Both can be graded by cut, colour, clarity, and carat weight.

The two can look very similar when they have comparable quality. Most buyers cannot tell the difference by looking at them. A trained jeweller may also not be able to identify origin by sight alone. Specialist testing and certification are used to confirm whether a diamond is natural or lab grown.

| Feature | Lab Grown Diamond | Natural Diamond |
| ----- | ----- | ----- |
| Real diamond? | Yes | Yes |
| Material | Carbon | Carbon |
| Origin | Laboratory-grown | Earth-formed |
| Certification | Available | Available |
| Appearance | Can look the same as natural diamonds | Depends on quality |
| Price | Usually more accessible | Usually higher |
| Resale expectation | Usually lower | Usually stronger |
| Best for | Value, size, certified beauty | Rarity, mined origin, tradition |

## **Are Lab Grown Diamonds the Same as Natural Diamonds?**

Lab grown diamonds are the same as natural diamonds in many important ways, but not in origin. Both are real diamonds, both are made of carbon, both can be polished into fine jewellery stones, and both can be graded by recognised laboratories.

However, they are not identical in market meaning. Natural diamonds are valued partly for rarity and geological origin. Lab grown diamonds are valued for being real diamonds with better price accessibility and modern sourcing. This difference affects price, resale value, and buyer preference.

| Same | Different |
| ----- | ----- |
| Both are real diamonds | Origin is different |
| Both are made of carbon | Natural diamonds are mined |
| Both can sparkle beautifully | Lab grown diamonds are created in laboratories |
| Both can be certified | Price structure is different |
| Both can be used in fine jewellery | Resale expectations are different |

## **Do Lab Grown Diamonds Look Real?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds look real because they are real diamonds. A well-cut lab grown diamond can have strong brilliance, fire, and sparkle. Its beauty depends on cut quality, proportions, colour, clarity, and polishing, not simply on whether it is lab grown.

A poorly cut lab grown diamond may not look beautiful, just as a poorly cut natural diamond may not look beautiful. The key is not only origin. The quality of the actual stone matters.

| Appearance Factor | Why It Matters |
| ----- | ----- |
| Cut quality | Controls sparkle and brilliance |
| Colour grade | Affects how white or warm the diamond appears |
| Clarity grade | Affects visible inclusions |
| Shape | Changes the overall look |
| Measurements | Affects face-up size |
| Polish and symmetry | Affect finish and light performance |

## **Do Lab Grown Diamonds Sparkle Like Real Diamonds?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds can sparkle like real diamonds because they are real diamonds. Their sparkle comes from how light moves through the stone. Cut quality, symmetry, polish, proportions, and shape all affect sparkle.

A round brilliant lab grown diamond with excellent cut can show strong brilliance. Oval, pear, radiant, cushion, and emerald cut diamonds each have different sparkle styles. The buyer should compare actual stones instead of assuming all lab grown diamonds look the same.

| Shape | Sparkle Style |
| ----- | ----- |
| Round | Classic strong brilliance |
| Oval | Bright and elegant with elongated look |
| Radiant | Strong sparkle with modern shape |
| Cushion | Soft romantic sparkle |
| Pear | Elegant sparkle with teardrop shape |
| Emerald | Step-cut reflections, less fiery but very refined |
| Marquise | Long shape with dramatic presence |

## **Do Lab Grown Diamonds Pass Diamond Testers?**

Many standard diamond testers identify lab grown diamonds as diamonds because they share diamond properties. However, a basic diamond tester may not tell whether the diamond is lab grown or natural. It may only confirm that the stone behaves like diamond.

To confirm origin, advanced gemological testing and certification are used. A grading report from a recognised laboratory is the best way to confirm whether a diamond is lab grown or natural.

| Test Question | Answer |
| ----- | ----- |
| Do lab grown diamonds test as diamonds? | Yes, many standard testers identify them as diamonds. |
| Can a basic tester identify lab grown origin? | Usually no. |
| How is origin confirmed? | Specialist testing and grading reports. |
| Should buyers rely only on a tester? | No, certification is better for important purchases. |

## **Can a Jeweller Tell a Lab Grown Diamond?**

A jeweller may not always be able to tell a lab grown diamond from a natural diamond by eye. Lab grown and natural diamonds can look nearly identical when they have similar quality. To confirm origin, jewellers rely on certification, laser inscriptions, and advanced testing equipment.

This is why a certificate is important when buying a lab grown diamond. A certificate makes the origin and specifications clear. It helps buyers avoid confusion and gives more confidence during comparison.

| Identification Method | Can It Confirm Lab Grown Origin? |
| ----- | ----- |
| Naked eye | Usually no |
| Standard loupe | Not always |
| Basic diamond tester | Usually confirms diamond, not origin |
| Advanced gemological equipment | Yes |
| Laboratory grading report | Yes |
| Laser inscription and report number | Helpful for verification |

## **How Are Lab Grown Diamonds Made?**

Lab grown diamonds are created using two main methods: CVD and HPHT. Both methods grow real diamond crystals, but they use different processes.

CVD stands for Chemical Vapour Deposition. In this method, a small diamond seed is placed in a chamber with carbon-rich gas. Carbon atoms build up on the seed, creating a diamond crystal layer by layer.

HPHT stands for High Pressure High Temperature. This method recreates the high pressure and high temperature conditions under which diamonds naturally form underground. A diamond seed grows into a larger crystal under controlled conditions.

| Method | Full Name | Simple Explanation |
| ----- | ----- | ----- |
| CVD | Chemical Vapour Deposition | Diamond grows from carbon-rich gas |
| HPHT | High Pressure High Temperature | Diamond grows under intense pressure and heat |

## **Is CVD Diamond Real?**

Yes, a CVD diamond is real diamond if it has grown as a diamond crystal. CVD is only the growth method. The final stone can be cut, polished, graded, and certified as a lab grown diamond.

A CVD diamond can be high quality or low quality depending on growth, cutting, polishing, colour, clarity, and treatment disclosure. Buyers should not choose only by growth method. They should check the certificate and full specifications.

## **Is HPHT Diamond Real?**

Yes, an HPHT diamond is real diamond if it has grown as a diamond crystal. HPHT is another method used to create lab grown diamonds. Like CVD diamonds, HPHT diamonds can be cut, polished, graded, and certified.

Both CVD and HPHT diamonds can be good choices. The better diamond is the one with better cut, colour, clarity, carat, proportions, certification, and overall appearance.

| Buyer Question | Best Answer |
| ----- | ----- |
| Is CVD diamond real? | Yes, CVD diamonds are real lab grown diamonds. |
| Is HPHT diamond real? | Yes, HPHT diamonds are real lab grown diamonds. |
| Is CVD better than HPHT? | Not always. Compare the actual diamond. |
| Is HPHT better than CVD? | Not always. Compare quality and certificate. |

## **Are Lab Grown Diamonds Certified?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds can be certified by recognised grading laboratories. A grading report helps confirm the diamond’s specifications and lab grown origin. It can include carat weight, colour, clarity, measurements, polish, symmetry, fluorescence, and other details.

Certification is especially important for loose lab grown diamonds, engagement ring stones, larger diamonds, and wholesale purchases. It gives buyers a professional record of what they are buying.

| Certificate Detail | Why It Matters |
| ----- | ----- |
| Lab grown origin | Confirms the diamond is laboratory-grown |
| Carat weight | Shows diamond weight |
| Colour grade | Helps compare whiteness |
| Clarity grade | Helps compare inclusions |
| Measurements | Shows actual size |
| Cut grade | Helps evaluate sparkle |
| Polish | Shows finishing quality |
| Symmetry | Shows precision |
| Report number | Allows verification |

## **IGI Certified Lab Grown Diamonds**

IGI certified lab grown diamonds are commonly searched because IGI is widely used in the lab grown diamond market. An IGI report can help buyers compare diamonds based on clear specifications instead of relying only on photos or seller descriptions.

For buyers comparing loose lab grown diamonds online, IGI certification is useful because it gives important grading details. This can make the buying process easier and more transparent.

| IGI Question | Answer |
| ----- | ----- |
| Are IGI certified lab grown diamonds real? | Yes, if the stone is graded as a lab grown diamond. |
| Is IGI certification useful? | Yes, it helps confirm specifications. |
| Can IGI certify loose lab diamonds? | Yes. |
| Should I verify the report number? | Yes, whenever possible. |

## **GIA Certified Lab Grown Diamonds**

GIA certified lab grown diamonds may also be available. GIA is a recognised name in diamond grading. Buyers who prefer GIA should check the actual report details and verify the report number when possible.

The most important point is that buyers should review the full certificate, not just the laboratory name. A certificate is useful only when the buyer understands what the report says.

| GIA Question | Answer |
| ----- | ----- |
| Can GIA certify lab grown diamonds? | Yes. |
| Is GIA recognised? | Yes, GIA is widely recognised. |
| Should I choose GIA or IGI? | It depends on buyer preference, availability, and report details. |
| Is a certified diamond better than non-certified? | Usually yes for important purchases. |

## **Are Lab Grown Diamonds Good Quality?**

Lab grown diamonds can be excellent quality, but not all lab grown diamonds are the same. Like natural diamonds, they vary by cut, colour, clarity, carat, shape, polish, symmetry, and overall appearance.

A high-quality lab grown diamond can look bright, clean, and beautiful. A lower-quality lab grown diamond may have poor proportions, visible inclusions, or weaker sparkle. This is why buyers should compare certified stones carefully.

| Quality Factor | What to Check |
| ----- | ----- |
| Cut | Most important for sparkle |
| Colour | How white or warm the diamond appears |
| Clarity | How clean the diamond looks |
| Carat | Weight and size category |
| Shape | Style and visual personality |
| Measurements | Face-up size and proportions |
| Certificate | Confirms grading details |

## **Are Lab Grown Diamonds Worth It?**

Lab grown diamonds can be worth it for buyers who want a real diamond, certified quality, larger size options, and better upfront value than natural diamonds. They are especially attractive for engagement rings, earrings, pendants, bracelets, and jewellery production.

However, buyers should understand resale value honestly. Lab grown diamonds usually have lower and less predictable resale value than natural diamonds. They are best purchased for beauty and jewellery use, not mainly as investments.

| Buyer Goal | Are Lab Grown Diamonds a Good Fit? |
| ----- | ----- |
| Real diamond | Yes |
| Larger size for budget | Yes |
| Certified loose stone | Yes |
| Engagement ring | Yes |
| Earrings or jewellery | Yes |
| Wholesale sourcing | Yes |
| Investment resale | Usually not the main reason |
| Natural rarity | Natural diamond may be preferred |

## **Do Lab Grown Diamonds Hold Value?**

Lab grown diamonds usually do not hold value the same way natural diamonds may. Their resale value can be lower and less predictable because production, supply, and market pricing can change.

This does not mean lab grown diamonds have no value. Their value is mainly in beauty, quality, certification, and wearability. If a buyer wants a diamond to wear and enjoy, lab grown diamonds can make sense. If resale is the main priority, the buyer should study the secondary market carefully.

## **Are Lab Grown Diamonds Ethical?**

Lab grown diamonds are often considered an alternative to mined diamonds because they do not require traditional diamond mining. This is one reason many buyers choose them.

However, ethical buying should still be handled carefully. Buyers should consider supplier transparency, energy use, production practices, certification, and honest disclosure. The best approach is to choose a supplier that clearly explains the diamond’s origin and specifications.

| Ethical Factor | Why It Matters |
| ----- | ----- |
| No traditional mining | Important for many buyers |
| Energy use | Production still requires energy |
| Supplier transparency | Helps buyers trust the source |
| Certification | Confirms origin and grading |
| Honest disclosure | Prevents confusion with natural diamonds |

## **Are Lab Grown Diamonds Good for Engagement Rings?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds are good for engagement rings. They are real diamonds and can be selected in many shapes, carat sizes, colours, and clarities. Many couples choose lab grown diamonds because they allow a larger centre stone or better specifications within budget.

Popular lab grown diamond engagement ring shapes include round, oval, emerald, cushion, pear, radiant, princess, and marquise. The best shape depends on personal style and setting design.

| Engagement Ring Priority | Why Lab Grown Diamonds Work |
| ----- | ----- |
| Real diamond centre stone | Lab grown diamonds are real diamonds |
| Larger carat size | More accessible than natural diamonds |
| Certified quality | Reports can confirm specifications |
| Custom design | Loose stones can be selected first |
| Modern buying preference | Appeals to many current buyers |
| Better upfront value | Strong size-for-budget potential |

## **Are Lab Grown Diamonds Good for Earrings?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds are good for earrings. They are especially useful for buyers who want larger studs, matched pairs, or diamond earrings at better value than natural diamond options.

For earrings, matching is important. The two diamonds should look balanced in size, colour, clarity, and sparkle. Lab grown diamonds can be selected for matching pairs and jewellery production.

| Earring Type | Why Lab Grown Diamonds Work |
| ----- | ----- |
| Stud earrings | Larger matched pairs for budget |
| Drop earrings | Elegant real diamond sparkle |
| Bridal earrings | Certified beauty for special occasions |
| Hoop earrings | Consistent stones for repeated settings |
| Statement earrings | Larger stones become more accessible |

## **Are Lab Grown Diamonds Good for Jewellery Businesses?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds can be useful for jewellers, retailers, designers, and manufacturers. They offer real diamond appeal with more accessible pricing and can be sourced as loose stones, matched pairs, melee diamonds, parcels, or certified stones.

For jewellery businesses, lab grown diamonds can help serve customers who want larger diamonds, modern sourcing, and certified options. Wholesale supply also matters because businesses often need consistency, availability, and clear specifications.

| Business Need | Lab Grown Diamond Use |
| ----- | ----- |
| Custom engagement rings | Certified loose stones |
| Earrings | Matched pairs |
| Bracelets | Parcels and melee diamonds |
| Retail inventory | Sellable certified diamonds |
| Jewellery production | Repeatable supply |
| Client requests | Specific carat, shape, colour, clarity |

## **How to Know If a Lab Grown Diamond Is Real**

The best way to know if a lab grown diamond is real is to check its certification and buy from a trusted supplier. The certificate should clearly state that the stone is a lab grown diamond and provide grading details.

Buyers should avoid relying only on photos, social media listings, or verbal claims. For important purchases, ask for the report number, full specifications, and confirmation of origin.

| Verification Step | Why It Matters |
| ----- | ----- |
| Ask for certificate | Confirms diamond details |
| Check report number | Helps verify the grading report |
| Review 4Cs | Confirms quality specifications |
| Confirm origin | Lab grown or natural should be clear |
| Check measurements | Helps compare size |
| Ask supplier questions | Reduces confusion |
| Avoid unclear listings | Prevents buying simulants by mistake |

## **Common Mistakes Buyers Make**

The biggest mistake is thinking lab grown means fake. Another mistake is assuming all lab grown diamonds are equal. Lab grown diamonds are real diamonds, but quality still varies.

Some buyers also compare lab grown diamonds with moissanite or cubic zirconia without understanding the difference. Moissanite and cubic zirconia are not diamonds. If the buyer wants a real diamond, they should choose a certified lab grown diamond or natural diamond.

| Mistake | Better Approach |
| ----- | ----- |
| Thinking lab grown diamonds are fake | Understand they are real diamonds with lab origin |
| Buying without certification | Ask for grading details |
| Comparing only price | Compare cut, colour, clarity, carat, and certificate |
| Confusing moissanite with lab diamond | Check the material and disclosure |
| Ignoring cut quality | Prioritise sparkle and proportions |
| Assuming all lab diamonds are identical | Compare actual stones |
| Not verifying report number | Check certificate details when possible |

## **Buyer Checklist: Are Lab Grown Diamonds Real?**

| Checklist Question | What to Confirm |
| ----- | ----- |
| Is the stone disclosed as lab grown diamond? | Yes |
| Is it made of diamond, not simulant? | Confirm through certificate |
| Does it have a grading report? | Preferably yes |
| Does the report state lab grown origin? | Yes |
| Are the 4Cs clearly listed? | Yes |
| Is the supplier transparent? | Yes |
| Is the price connected to real specifications? | Yes |
| Is the diamond suitable for the intended jewellery? | Yes |

Whether you are checking if lab grown diamonds are real, comparing certified loose lab diamonds, looking for current lab grown diamond prices, or sourcing stones for jewellery production, Uniglo Diamonds can help you explore available options with clarity.

# **Are Lab Grown Diamonds Real? FAQs**

## **Basic FAQs**

### **Are lab grown diamonds real?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds are real diamonds. They are made of carbon and have diamond properties. Their origin is laboratory-grown instead of earth-mined.

### **Are lab grown diamonds fake?**

No, lab grown diamonds are not fake. They are real diamonds created in controlled laboratory conditions.

### **Are lab grown diamonds natural?**

No, lab grown diamonds are not natural diamonds. They are real diamonds, but they are grown in a laboratory instead of forming underground.

### **Are lab grown diamonds synthetic?**

Lab grown diamonds are sometimes called synthetic diamonds because they are created by technology. However, this does not mean they are fake. They are real diamonds with lab-grown origin.

### **Are lab grown diamonds man-made?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds are man-made diamonds. They are created in controlled laboratory environments using advanced technology.

### **Are lab diamonds real diamonds?**

Yes, lab diamonds are real diamonds. “Lab diamonds” is simply a shorter term for lab grown diamonds.

### **Are lab created diamonds real?**

Yes, lab created diamonds are real diamonds. Lab created diamond and lab grown diamond usually mean the same thing.

### **Are cultured diamonds real?**

Yes, cultured diamonds usually refer to lab grown diamonds, which are real diamonds created in controlled conditions.

## **Diamond Tester FAQs**

### **Do lab grown diamonds pass a diamond tester?**

Many standard diamond testers identify lab grown diamonds as diamonds because they share diamond properties. However, specialist testing is needed to confirm origin.

### **Do lab grown diamonds test as real?**

Yes, many lab grown diamonds test as real diamonds on standard diamond testers. A tester may not show whether the diamond is natural or lab grown.

### **Can a jeweller tell a lab grown diamond?**

A jeweller may not always be able to tell by eye alone. Certification and advanced testing are used to confirm origin.

### **How can you tell if a diamond is lab grown?**

The best way is to check the grading report and use advanced gemological testing. A certificate should clearly state lab grown origin.

### **Can lab grown diamonds be detected?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds can be detected using specialist equipment and laboratory testing.

### **Do lab grown diamonds have laser inscriptions?**

Many certified lab grown diamonds may have laser inscriptions linked to their grading report. Buyers should check the certificate details.

## **Comparison FAQs**

### **Are lab grown diamonds the same as natural diamonds?**

They are both real diamonds, but their origin is different. Lab grown diamonds are created in a laboratory, while natural diamonds form underground.

### **Are lab grown diamonds as good as natural diamonds?**

Lab grown diamonds can be as beautiful as natural diamonds when they have strong cut, colour, clarity, and certification. The better choice depends on buyer priorities.

### **Are lab grown diamonds better than natural diamonds?**

They are better for buyers who want a real diamond with better size-for-budget. Natural diamonds may be better for buyers who want rarity and mined origin.

### **Are natural diamonds better than lab grown diamonds?**

Natural diamonds may be better for buyers who value natural rarity, tradition, and stronger resale perception. Lab grown diamonds may be better for value and size.

### **Are lab grown diamonds the same as moissanite?**

No, lab grown diamonds are not moissanite. Moissanite is a different gemstone made of silicon carbide.

### **Are lab grown diamonds cubic zirconia?**

No, lab grown diamonds are not cubic zirconia. Cubic zirconia is a diamond simulant, not a real diamond.

### **Are lab grown diamonds glass?**

No, lab grown diamonds are not glass. They are real diamonds made of carbon.

## **Quality FAQs**

### **Do lab grown diamonds sparkle?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds sparkle like diamonds when they are well cut and properly polished.

### **Do lab grown diamonds shine like real diamonds?**

Yes, because they are real diamonds. Their shine depends on cut quality, proportions, and cleanliness.

### **Do lab grown diamonds get cloudy?**

A properly grown and cut lab grown diamond does not become cloudy simply because it is lab grown. Like all jewellery, it should be cleaned regularly.

### **Do lab grown diamonds last forever?**

Lab grown diamonds are highly durable and can last for generations with proper care and secure setting.

### **Can lab grown diamonds chip?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds can chip if hit hard in the wrong way, just like natural diamonds.

### **Are lab grown diamonds good quality?**

Lab grown diamonds can be excellent quality, but quality varies. Buyers should check cut, colour, clarity, carat, certificate, and measurements.

### **Are all lab grown diamonds the same?**

No, lab grown diamonds vary by shape, carat, cut, colour, clarity, certificate, and overall appearance.

## **Certification FAQs**

### **Can lab grown diamonds be certified?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds can be certified by recognised grading laboratories.

### **Should lab grown diamonds be certified?**

For important purchases, certification is strongly recommended because it confirms origin and grading details.

### **What is an IGI certified lab grown diamond?**

An IGI certified lab grown diamond is a lab grown diamond graded by the International Gemological Institute.

### **What is a GIA certified lab grown diamond?**

A GIA certified lab grown diamond is a lab grown diamond graded by GIA. Buyers should review the report details before purchase.

### **Is IGI certification good for lab grown diamonds?**

IGI certification is widely used in the lab grown diamond market and helps buyers compare specifications.

### **Is GIA certification good for lab grown diamonds?**

GIA is a recognised grading authority. Buyers who prefer GIA should check the actual report information and availability.

### **Can I verify a lab grown diamond certificate?**

Yes, many grading reports can be verified using the report number on the grading laboratory’s official verification system.

## **Price and Value FAQs**

### **Are lab grown diamonds cheaper?**

Lab grown diamonds are usually more affordable than natural diamonds with similar visible specifications.

### **Why are lab grown diamonds cheaper?**

They are usually cheaper because they are created in controlled production environments and do not carry the same natural rarity premium as mined diamonds.

### **Are lab grown diamonds worth it?**

Lab grown diamonds can be worth it for buyers who want a real diamond, certified quality, larger size, and better upfront value.

### **Do lab grown diamonds hold value?**

Lab grown diamonds usually have lower and less predictable resale value than natural diamonds.

### **Are lab grown diamonds worthless?**

No, lab grown diamonds are not worthless. They are real diamonds, but resale value may be lower than the original purchase price.

### **Are lab grown diamonds a good investment?**

Lab grown diamonds are usually not bought mainly as investments. They are better bought for beauty, jewellery use, and value at purchase.

### **Why do lab grown diamonds lose value?**

Lab grown diamonds may lose resale value because production, technology, supply, and market pricing can change.

## **Engagement Ring FAQs**

### **Are lab grown diamonds good for engagement rings?**

Yes, lab grown diamonds are good for engagement rings because they are real diamonds and can offer better size-for-budget than natural diamonds.

### **Is a lab grown diamond engagement ring real?**

Yes, a lab grown diamond engagement ring has a real diamond centre stone if the stone is properly disclosed as lab grown diamond.

### **Will people know my engagement ring is lab grown?**

Most people cannot tell by looking. Lab grown and natural diamonds can look almost identical when similarly graded.

### **Is it okay to propose with a lab grown diamond?**

Yes, many couples choose lab grown diamonds for engagement rings because they are real diamonds and offer strong value.

### **Are lab grown diamond rings less valuable?**

They may have lower resale value than natural diamond rings, but they can still be valuable as fine jewellery and meaningful engagement rings.

### **Should I tell someone the diamond is lab grown?**

Yes, diamond origin should always be disclosed clearly and honestly.

## **Buying FAQs**

### **Should I buy a lab grown diamond?**

You should buy a lab grown diamond if you want a real diamond, certified quality, better size-for-budget, and modern sourcing.

### **What should I check before buying a lab grown diamond?**

Check shape, carat, cut, colour, clarity, certificate, report number, measurements, polish, symmetry, price, and supplier trust.

### **Where can I buy real lab grown diamonds?**

You can buy real lab grown diamonds from a supplier that provides certified stones, clear specifications, current availability, and support before purchase.

### **Can I buy loose lab grown diamonds?**

Yes, loose lab grown diamonds are available for engagement rings, earrings, pendants, bracelets, custom jewellery, and wholesale sourcing.

### **Can jewellers buy lab grown diamonds wholesale?**

Yes, jewellers, retailers, designers, and manufacturers can buy lab grown diamonds wholesale for jewellery production and resale.

### **How do I know if I am buying a real lab grown diamond?**

Ask for a certificate, check the report number, review the 4Cs, confirm the diamond origin, and buy from a transparent supplier.

## **Final Summary**

Lab grown diamonds are real diamonds. They are made of carbon, can be certified, and can be used in fine jewellery just like natural diamonds. They are not fake diamonds, moissanite, cubic zirconia, glass, or imitation stones.

The main difference is origin. Natural diamonds form underground, while lab grown diamonds are created in controlled laboratory conditions. For buyers who want a real diamond with better size-for-budget, clear certification, and modern sourcing, lab grown diamonds can be an excellent choice.

Uniglo Diamonds helps buyers source certified lab grown diamonds, loose stones, matched pairs, and wholesale options with clear specifications and professional support.
